(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
AVTS2 VIRTUAL LIFESTYLE PRIVATE LIMITED
No. 60, Marshalls Road, Egmore, Chennai – 600 008
CIN:U93000TN2013PTC092447
Notice is hereby given that the Members of AVTS2 VIRTUAL LIFESTYLE PRIVATE LIMITED at their Extra-ordinary
General Meeting held on TUESDAY, the 16th JUNE, 2015 at 11.00 A.M. at No. 60, RUKMANI LAKSHMIPATHI SALAI,
EGMORE, CHENNAI – 600 008 have passed the following Special Resolution to wind up the above company voluntarily.
1.

Members Voluntary Winding up

“RESOLVED THAT pursuant to the provisions of section 484(1) (b) of the Companies Act, 1956, the consent of the
members of the Company be and is hereby accorded to wind up the affairs of the Company as the members Voluntary
Winding up, w.e.f 31st March, 2015”.
2.

Appointment of Liquidator

“RESOLVED that pursuant to the provision of Section 490 of the Companies Act, 1956, consent of the Members be
and is hereby accorded to appoint Mr. V. Suresh, Practising Company Secretary, (Regn. No. C.P. 6032) # 28, Ganapathy
Colony, 3rd Street, Teynampet, Chennai – 600 018, as Liquidator of the Company at a remuneration of Rs.1,00,000/(Rupees One Lakh Only) excluding the payment of Service Tax and reimbursement of out of pocket expenses”.

Chennai,
24th June 2015.

V. SURESH,
Liquidator.
